if (is_file('img/arrow_back.png') && (sha1_file('img/arrow_back.png') != '1f0e550b1140c3766f455a6c29510910669f3271')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: img/arrow_back.png');
	$tmp = pathinfo('img/arrow_back.png');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('img/arrow_back.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('img/arrow_back.png', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('img/arrow_back.png')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): img/arrow_back.png');
} else if (sha1_file('img/arrow_back.png') != '1f0e550b1140c3766f455a6c29510910669f3271') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): img/arrow_back.png');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('img/arrow_back.png', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of img/arrow_back.png');
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') != '1ed8d86e33fc6e5d639bcdbf8a333f0368819571') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== '1ed8d86e33fc6e5d639bcdbf8a333f0368819571') {

			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();

if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php') != 'cc815f7fb34e96e6448e2f0eb1b9a97f27f3ec16') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php') !== 'cc815f7fb34e96e6448e2f0eb1b9a97f27f3ec16') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php') !== '6fe54db370fd4062466d58c2913eb784d0324d92') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php') !== 'cc815f7fb34e96e6448e2f0eb1b9a97f27f3ec16') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: index.php');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index.php') != '6b3c410cad5db5a2777dbce2a0ad7f13a56abcf3') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '6b3c410cad5db5a2777dbce2a0ad7f13a56abcf3') {
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '7aab4117bf98b4ef7a9e5c54a80eb1977a4f0d49') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '6b3c410cad5db5a2777dbce2a0ad7f13a56abcf3') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('oidplus.js')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: oidplus.js');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('oidplus.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus.js') != '64cac18b348da61e3a3f0603e393c3940079071e') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus.js') !== '64cac18b348da61e3a3f0603e393c3940079071e') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.js') !== '7f31486c954de8ea6bd3d93cb05008bb45910501') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.js') !== '64cac18b348da61e3a3f0603e393c3940079071e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus.js');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 127\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 127') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
